<script>
    (async function () {

        async function loadScript(src) {
            return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
                const script = document.createElement('script');
                script.src = src;
                script.onload = () => resolve();
                script.onerror = () => reject(new Error(`failed ${src}`));
